                                                                                                                          On Atmospheric Electricity — Of Fall

                                                                                                                            —Of         Waterspouts      and   Whirl

                                                                                                                            CHARLES.          Does the air always
                                                                                                                          contain electricity?
                                                                                                                            Tutor.     Yes ; and it is owing to the
Public Domain, Google-digitized / http://www.hathitrust.org/access_use#pd-google
                                                                                                                          electricity of the atmosphere that we
                                                                                                                          observe    a    number of curious      and
                                                                                                                          interesting    phenomena, such as fall
                                                                                                                          ing stars ; the aurora borealis, or north

                                                                                                                                     FALLING STARS.                135
                                                                                                                          ern lights; the ignis fatuus, or       Will-
                                                                                                                          with-the-wisp.                                 >
                                                                                                                            James.    I    have     frequently   seen
                                                                                                                          what people call falling stars, but        I
                                                                                                                          never knew that they were occasioned
                                                                                                                          merely by electricity.
                                                                                                                            Tutor.    These are seen chiefly in
                                                                                                                          clear and calm weather:         it is then
                                                                                                                          that the electric fluid is probably not
Generated for acobblah (University of Michigan) on 2015-08-10 15:18 GMT / http://hdl.handle.net/2027/hvd.32044102874112
                                                                                                                          very strong, and passing through the
                                                                                                                          air it becomes      visible in particular
                                                                                                                          parts of its passage, according to the
                                                                                                                          conducting substances it may meet
                                                                                                                          with.   One of the most striking phe
                                                                                                                          nomena of this kind is recorded by
                                                                                                                          Signior Beccaria.   — As    he was sitting
                                                                                                                          with a friend     in the open air,       an
Public Domain, Google-digitized / http://www.hathitrust.org/access_use#pd-google
                                                                                                                          hour after sun-set, they saw a fall
                                                                                                                          ing, or, as it is sometimes called, a
                                                                                                                          shooting star, directing its course to
                                                                                                                                              N 2

                                                                                                                          130            ELECTRICITY.
                                                                                                                          wards      them,      growing-,      apparently,
                                                                                                                          larger and larger, till it disappeared
                                                                                                                          not far from them, and, disappearing,
                                                                                                                          it left their faces, hands, and clothes,
                                                                                                                          with the earth and neighbouring ob
                                                                                                                          jects,     suddenly     illuminated with       a
                                                                                                                          diffused and lambent light, attended
                                                                                                                          with no noise at all.
                                                                                                                             Charles.        But how did he know
Generated for acobblah (University of Michigan) on 2015-08-10 15:18 GMT / http://hdl.handle.net/2027/hvd.32044102874112

                                                                                                                          tricity?

                                                                                                                          raised his kite, and found the air very

                                                                                                                                Miscellaneous Experiments.
                                                                                                                            TUTOR. The             discoveries of   Gal-
                                                                                                                          yani were made principally with dead
                                                                                                                          frogs;   from     his     experiments,    and
                                                                                                                          many     others that have heen           made
                                                                                                                          since his time, it appears that the
                                                                                                                          nerves   of animals     may be affected by
                                                                                                                          smaller quantities of electricity than
Public Domain, Google-digitized / http://www.hathitrust.org/access_use#pd-google
                                                                                                                          any other substances with which we
                                                                                                                          are acquainted.         Hence limbs of ani
                                                                                                                          mals, properly prepared,         have been

                                                                                                                                        EXPERIMENTS.                     213
                                                                                                                          much employed for ascertaining the
                                                                                                                          Voltaic electricity.
                                                                                                                             Charles.       What is the method of
                                                                                                                          preparation   ?              ^
                                                                                                                             Tutor.     I   have been          cautious in
                                                                                                                          mentioning experiments on animals,
                                                                                                                          lest    they should    lead you to trifle
                                                                                                                          with their feelings:             I   must, how
Generated for acobblah (University of Michigan) on 2015-08-10 15:19 GMT / http://hdl.handle.net/2027/hvd.32044102874112
                                                                                                                          ever, to    render     the        subject   more
                                                                                                                          complete,     tell you what           has    been
                                                                                                                          done.
                                                                                                                             The muscles of    lately dead,
                                                                                                                                                 a frog
                                                                                                                          and skinned, may be brought into
                                                                                                                          action by means of very small quanti
                                                                                                                          ties of common electricity.
                                                                                                                             If   the leg   of a frog recently         dead
                                                                                                                          be prepared, that      is,       separated from
Public Domain, Google-digitized / http://www.hathitrust.org/access_use#pd-google
                                                                                                                          the rest of the body, having a small
                                                                                                                          portion of the spine attached to                it,
                                                                                                                          and so situated that    a        little electricity

                                                                                                                          214                   VOLTATSM.
                                                                                                                          may pass through             it,   the leg     will be
                                                                                                                          instantly affected            with       a     kind   of
                                                                                                                          spasmodic           contraction, sometimes            so
                                                                                                                          strong        as    to   jump      a   considerable
                                                                                                                          distance.
                                                                                                                             It    is    now known           that similar       ef
                                                                                                                          fects    may be produced               in    the limb
                                                                                                                          thus     prepared,        by only        making        a
                                                                                                                          communication             between        the    nerves
Generated for acobblah (University of Michigan) on 2015-08-10 15:19 GMT / http://hdl.handle.net/2027/hvd.32044102874112
                                                                                                                          and     the muscles,            by
                                                                                                                                                           conducting
                                                                                                                                                               a
                                                                                                                          substance.           Thus, in an animal rer
                                                                                                                          cently dead,         if  a   nerve be detached
                                                                                                                          from the surrounding parts and the       ;
                                                                                                                          coverings be removed from over the
                                                                                                                          muscles, which depend on that nerve                   ;
                                                                                                                          and     if   a     piece of metal, as          a   wire,
                                                                                                                          touch        the nerve with one extremity,
Public Domain, Google-digitized / http://www.hathitrust.org/access_use#pd-google
                                                                                                                          and the muscle with the other, the
                                                                                                                          limb will be convulsed.

                                                                                                                                        EXPERIMENTS.                     215
                                                                                                                             Charles.     Is it necessary that           the
                                                                                                                          communication between the nerve and
                                                                                                                          the muscle should        be made with a
